HTTP Security Headers\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/security-headers.ts`\n\n**Headers Configured:**\n- **Content-Security-Policy (CSP):** Level 3, with nonce support for strict mode\n  - `default-src 'self'`\n  - `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'` (can upgrade to nonce-based)\n  - `style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'`\n  - `img-src 'self' data: https:`\n  - `connect-src 'self'`\n  - `object-src 'none'` (prevents plugin exploitation)\n  - `base-uri 'self'` (prevents base tag injection)\n  - `form-action 'self'` (prevents form hijacking)\n  - `frame-ancestors 'none'` (prevents clickjacking)\n  - `upgrade-insecure-requests` (HTTPS enforcement)\n  - Report-URI/Report-to for violation monitoring\n  \n- **X-Content-Type-Options:** `nosniff` (MIME type sniffing prevention)\n- **X-Frame-Options:** `DENY` (clickjacking prevention)\n- **Referrer-Policy:** `strict-origin-when-cross-origin` (privacy-preserving)\n- **Strict-Transport-Security:** `max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains; preload` (HTTPS enforcement)\n- **Permissions-Policy:** Blocks geolocation, camera, microphone, payment, USB, magnetometer, gyroscope, accelerometer, ambient-light-sensor\n- **Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy:** `same-origin` (prevents window.opener access)\n- **Cross-Origin-Resource-Policy:** `same-origin` (restricts CORS resource access)\n- **Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy:** `require-corp` (Spectre mitigation)\n- **X-Permitted-Cross-Domain-Policies:** `none` (Adobe Flash/PDF hardening)\n- **X-XSS-Protection:** `1; mode=block` (legacy browser support)\n\n#### B. Input Validation & Sanitization\n**Locations:** \n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/input-sanitization.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/sanitization.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/shared/src/utils/security.ts`\n\n**Protections:**\n- **Request validation:** Zod schemas for all endpoints (emptyQuerySchema, stationIdParamsSchema, etc.)\n- **Parameter validation:** `validateParams()`, `validateQuery()`, `validateBody()`\n- **Input sanitization:** Query string, form data, JSON body sanitization\n- **Output encoding functions:**\n  - `encodeHtml()` - HTML context XSS prevention\n  - `encodeHtmlAttribute()` - HTML attribute context\n  - `encodeJs()` - JavaScript string context\n  - `encodeUrl()` - URL parameter encoding\n  - `encodeCss()` - CSS string encoding\n  - `sanitizeHtml()` - Strip all tags\n  - `sanitizeUrl()` - Block javascript:/data: protocols\n  - `containsDangerousContent()` - XSS pattern detection\n  - `stripControlCharacters()` - Log injection prevention\n- **Mass assignment protection:** Field-level filtering (PUSH_SUBSCRIPTION_FIELDS, TRIP_NOTES_FIELDS, etc.)\n\n#### C. Authentication & Authorization\n**Locations:**\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/authentication.ts` (3000+ lines)\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/authorization.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/rbac.ts`\n\n**Authentication Features:**\n- **API Key Management:** Cryptographic generation (256-bit entropy), PBKDF2-SHA256 hashing (600k iterations per OWASP 2024)\n- **Password Management:**\n  - PBKDF2-SHA256 with 600,000 iterations\n  - Password breach detection (hibp.com integration)\n  - Password expiration (configurable by role)\n  - Password history enforcement (no reuse)\n  - Secure password generation\n  - Password pepper support (defense-in-depth)\n  - Grace period for expired passwords\n- **JWT Validation:** Full JWT validation with structure checks, replay detection\n- **Session Management:**\n  - Secure session regeneration\n  - Sliding expiration windows\n  - Concurrent session limits with device fingerprinting\n  - Session cleanup daemon (runs every 5 minutes)\n  - IP binding and geolocation checks\n  - Impossible travel detection\n- **Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA):** TOTP-based implementation\n- **Token Encryption:** AES-256-GCM with key derivation (PBKDF2)\n- **Token Revocation:** Revocation tracking and cleanup\n\n**Authorization Features:**\n- **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC):**\n  - Admin, User, Readonly roles\n  - Resource-level permissions (trips, subscriptions, journal)\n  - Action-based permissions (create, read, update, delete)\n  - Dynamic cache for permission lookups\n- **Resource Access:** `requireResourceAccess()`, `requireOwnershipOrAdmin()`\n- **Audit Trail:** All auth operations logged with user context\n\n#### D. Request Protection\n**Locations:** \n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/rate-limiter.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/request-limits.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/response-size-limits.ts`\n\n**Protections:**\n- **Rate Limiting:** Token bucket algorithm, 60 requests/min per IP, automatic bucket pruning\n- **Request Size Limits:** Configurable max body/header sizes (DoS protection)\n- **Response Size Limits:** Pagination support, stream response handling\n- **HTTP Method Restrictions:** Only GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE allowed; TRACE and CONNECT blocked\n- **HTTP Request Smuggling Protection:** Detects Transfer-Encoding/Content-Length conflicts\n- **HTTP Response Splitting Protection:** CRLF injection detection\n- **Host Header Protection:** \n  - Production-only IP/localhost blocking\n  - Allowed hosts whitelist (ALLOWED_HOSTS env var)\n  - Private network blocking in production\n- **HTTP Parameter Pollution (HPP) Protection:** First-value strategy for duplicate parameters\n- **JSON Depth Protection:** Prevents DoS via deeply nested JSON\n\n#### E. CSRF & Same-Origin Protection\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/csrf-protection.ts`\n\n**Features:**\n- **Cryptographically secure CSRF tokens** (Uint8Array + hex encoding)\n- **Token validation** on state-changing operations (POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE)\n- **SameSite=Strict** cookie attribute by default\n- **Per-endpoint exclusions:** Health, metrics, VAPID key, CSP reports, password reset exempt\n- **Same-origin verification** for push subscriptions and trip tracking\n\n#### F. Additional Security Middleware\n**Files & Protections:**\n- `open-redirect.ts` - Redirect URL validation, blocks javascript:/data: protocols\n- `path-traversal.ts` - Path traversal attack prevention (../, etc.)\n- `ssrf-protection.ts` - Server-Side Request Forgery protection, MTA feed allowlist\n- `dependency-security.ts` - Dependency vulnerability audit (OWASP 2024 recommendations)\n- `subresource-integrity.ts` - SRI hash generation and validation\n- `header-validation.ts` - Strict header name/value validation\n- `content-type.ts` - Content-Type validation and enforcement\n- `cors.ts` - CORS policy enforcement\n- `suspicious-activity-notifications.ts` - Security event notifications and rate limiting\n- `concurrent-session-management.ts` - Device fingerprinting, concurrent session limits\n- `enhanced-jwt-security.ts` - Token usage tracking, compromise detection\n- `session-security.ts` - Risk assessment, device trust levels, impossible travel\n- `token-encryption.ts` - Token encryption/decryption with key rotation\n- `cookie-security.ts` - Secure cookie signing and management\n- `auth-rate-limit.ts` - Authentication-specific rate limiting with IP banning\n- `captcha.ts` - CAPTCHA challenge integration (reCAPTCHA, hCaptcha support)\n- `audit-log.ts` - Comprehensive audit logging with filtering and export\n- `structured-audit-log.ts` - Enhanced audit with severity levels and compliance reporting\n- `admin-operations.ts` - Admin action audit and enforcement\n- `authorization-security.ts` - Time-based and location-based access rules\n- `enhanced-authentication.ts` - Advanced auth features (additional verification)\n- `api-key-management.ts` - API key creation/revocation with metadata tracking\n- `password-management.ts` - Password policy enforcement, reset token lifecycle\n\n#### G. Startup Security Validation\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/security-startup.ts`\n\n**Checks:**\n- **ALLOWED_HOSTS validation** (required in production, optional in dev)\n- **PASSWORD_PEPPER validation** (recommended, minimum 32 bytes / 64 hex chars)\n- **VAPID keys validation** (required for push notifications)\n- **Fail-fast startup** on critical security misconfigurations\n\n#### H. Logging & Monitoring\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/security-logging.ts`\n\n**Events Logged:**\n- Authentication failures (invalid credentials)\n- Authorization failures (permission denied)\n- Rate limit exceeded\n- Blocked attacks (XSS, CSRF, smuggling)\n- CSP violations\n- Admin operations\n- Data access (audit trail)\n\n#### I. Container Security\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/Dockerfile`\n\n**Security Features:**\n- **Non-root user:** Runs as `node` user (line 64)\n- **Multi-stage build:** Separates build from runtime dependencies\n- **Production dependencies only:** `npm ci --omit=dev` (line 45)\n- **Health checks:** HTTPS healthcheck endpoint (lines 68-69)\n- **Data directory permissions:** `chown -R node:node` for SQLite access (line 58)\n- **Minimal base image:** `node:22-slim` for reduced attack surface\n\n#### J. Security Gaps & Recommendations\n\n#### Minor Gaps:\n\n1. **CSP Relaxations for Development**\n   - `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'` allows all inline scripts\n   - **Recommendation:** Use nonce-based CSP for strict enforcement (`useStrictCSP: true` option exists but not enabled by default)\n\n2. **Rate Limiter Persistence**\n   - In-memory token buckets reset on pod restart\n   - **Recommendation:** Use Cloudflare WAF as documented; acceptable for single-container deployments\n   - **Code Comment:** \"Cloudflare WAF is the first line of defense; this is the second\"\n\n3. **Test Mode Bypass**\n   - `TEST_MODE=true` disables rate limiting\n   - **Recommendation:** Ensure this is never enabled in production (startup validation should catch it)\n\n4. **Password Pepper Optional**\n   - Recommended but not enforced\n   - **Recommendation:** Security startup warns but doesn't fail; good for flexibility\n\n5. **VAPID Keys Missing**\n   - Won't prevent server startup\n   - **Recommendation:** Push notifications won't work, but non-critical\n\n#### No Critical Security Gaps Found\n\nThe codebase demonstrates **enterprise-grade security hardening** across:\n- ✅ All OWASP Top 10 protections implemented\n- ✅ Comprehensive input validation and output encoding\n- ✅ Strong authentication and authorization\n- ✅ Rate limiting and DoS protection\n- ✅ Security logging and monitoring\n- ✅ Container hardening\n- ✅ Secure defaults (fail-fast validation)\n\n---\n\n### 5. Request Protection\n**Locations:** \n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/rate-limiter.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/request-limits.ts`\n- `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/response-size-limits.ts`\n\n**Protections:**\n- **Rate Limiting:** Token bucket algorithm, 60 requests/min per IP, automatic bucket pruning\n- **Request Size Limits:** Configurable max body/header sizes (DoS protection)\n- **Response Size Limits:** Pagination support, stream response handling\n- **HTTP Method Restrictions:** Only GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE allowed; TRACE and CONNECT blocked\n- **HTTP Request Smuggling Protection:** Detects Transfer-Encoding/Content-Length conflicts\n- **HTTP Response Splitting Protection:** CRLF injection detection\n- **Host Header Protection:** \n  - Production-only IP/localhost blocking\n  - Allowed hosts whitelist (ALLOWED_HOSTS env var)\n  - Private network blocking in production\n- **HTTP Parameter Pollution (HPP) Protection:** First-value strategy for duplicate parameters\n- **JSON Depth Protection:** Prevents DoS via deeply nested JSON\n\n#### E. CSRF & Same-Origin Protection\n**Location:** `/home/coding/mta-my-way/packages/server/src/middleware/csrf-protection.ts`\n\n**Features:**\n- **Cryptographically secure CSRF tokens** (Uint8Array + hex encoding)\n- **Token validation** on state-changing operations (POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE)\n- **SameSite=Strict** cookie attribute by default\n- **Per-endpoint exclusions:** Health, metrics, VAPID key, CSP reports, password reset exempt\n- **Same-origin verification** for push subscriptions and trip tracking\n\n#### F. Security Gaps & Recommendations\n\n#### Minor Gaps:\n\n1. **CSP Relaxations for Development**\n   - `script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'` allows all inline scripts\n   - **Recommendation:** Use nonce-based CSP for strict enforcement (`useStrictCSP: true` option exists but not enabled by default)\n\n2. **Rate Limiter Persistence**\n   - In-memory token buckets reset on pod restart\n   - **Recommendation:** Use Cloudflare WAF as documented; acceptable for single-container deployments\n   - **Code Comment:** \"Cloudflare WAF is the first line of defense; this is the second\"\n\n3. **Test Mode Bypass**\n   - `TEST_MODE=true` disables rate limiting\n   - **Recommendation:** Ensure this is never enabled in production (startup validation should catch it)\n\n4. **Password Pepper Optional**\n   - Recommended but not enforced\n   - **Recommendation:** Security startup warns but doesn't fail; good for flexibility\n\n5. **VAPID Keys Missing**\n   - Won't prevent server startup\n   - **Recommendation:** Push notifications won't work, but non-critical\n\n#### No Critical Security Gaps Found\n\nThe codebase demonstrates **enterprise-grade security hardening** across:\n- ✅ All OWASP Top 10 protections implemented\n- ✅ Comprehensive input validation and output encoding\n- ✅ Strong authentication and authorization\n- ✅ Rate limiting and DoS protection\n- ✅ Security logging and monitoring\n- ✅ Container hardening\n- ✅ Secure defaults (fail-fast validation)\n\n---\n\n### 5. Update the test for \"can be used to log events without creating a new instance\" to check the structured logger output format\n\nWhen using `logger.warn(\"security_event\", event as Record<string, unknown>)`:\n- The output (via console.warn internally in logger) would be: `JSON.stringify({ level: \"warn\", message: \"security_event\", timestamp: \"...\", context: { event: \"auth_failure\", ... } })`\n\n\n- So `loggedEvent.context.event` would be \"auth_failure\"\n\nI need to account for the fact that the `SecurityEvent` object has its own timestamp field, and the logger adds another one.
